\num{3} \eng{V} AkArada vasutx.
\num{4} roVmanf saMKAyx saMkeVtadalilx aidu.}

\eentry

\bentry
\word{vacancy} 
\pron{veVkanisx} 
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{vacancies}).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} baridAgiruvike; KAliyAgiruvike.
\num{2} shUnayxmanasakxte; jDamanasakxte; manasisxna niSikxrXya
sithxti. 
\num{3} KAli hudedx yA sAthxna: \eng{he has no vacancy on his staff}
Atana sibabxMdi vagaRdalilx yAva KAli sAthxnavU illx. \eng{no
 vacancies at present in this office} sadayxdalilx I kaceVriyalilx
yAva hudedxgaLU KAli illx. 
\num{4} (hoVTelu \mo vugaLalilx) lBayxviruva KAli koVNe, rUmu.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word{vacant} 
\pron{veVkaMTf} 
\gl{\gu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} baridAgiruva; KAli(yAgiruva); BatiRyAgillxda: \eng{the house
 is still vacant} A mane inUnx KAli ide. 
\num{2} biDuvAgiruva; yAva kelsavU illxde virAmavAgiruva: \eng{this
 will amuse your vacant hours} ninanx biDuvAda, 
virAmada, hotitxnalilx idu ninage vinoVdavanunx koDutatxde. 
\num{3} terapAgiruva; KAli iruva: \eng{he applied for a vacant post}
avanu terapAgidadx, KAli idadx, oMdu hudedxgAgi ajiR 
hAkikoMDa.
\num{4} shUnayxmanasakxnAda; vicAra, BAva -- shUnayx Ada; niSikxrXya,
jDa -- manasakxnAda: \eng{his mind seems completely vacant} 
avanu saMpUNRvAgi shUnayxmanasakxnaMtidAdxne. \eng{a vacant stare}
shUnayxdaqSiTx; gamanakekx tegedukoLaLxde neTTx daqSiTxyiMda 
elolxV noVDutitxruvudu.} 
\eentry

saMpUNRvAgi tegaduhAkibiTiTxruva pAterx yA parxdeVsha: 
\eng{Torricellian vacuum} TAriceliyanf nivARtaparxdeVsha. 
\num{3} vAyuviraLate; vAyuvina otatxDa yA saMmadaR sAmAnayxvAgi
irabeVkAda parxmANkikxMta kaDimeyAgiruvudu. 
\num{4} aBAva; rAhitayx; yAvudeV sathxLa, saninxveVsha, \mo vugaLalilx
irabeVkAda vayxkitx, vasutx, caTuvaTike, 
\mo vu illxdiruvudu.

\bentry
\word{vague} 
\pron{veVgf} 
\gl{\gu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} asapxSaTx; sapxSaTxvAgi, nidiRSaTxvAgi -- heVLillxda; asuPxT:
\eng{he returned only a vague answer} avanu 
EnoV oMdu asapxSaTxvAda utatxra koTTx, aSeTx. \eng{I have not the
 vaguest notion of reasons} avana kAraNgaLeVnu eMba 
bagegx nanage tiVra asapxSaTxvAda BAvane kUDa illx. \eng{I heard a
 vague rumour to that effect} A athaR baruva yAvudoV 
oMdu asapxSaTx vadaMti nananx kivige bitutx.

\bentry
\word[variable(1)]{variable} 
\pron{veVriabflf} 
\gl{\gu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (beVkAda riVti) badalAyisabahudAda; mApaRDisabahudAda;
hoMdisikoLaLxbahudAda; vayxtAyxsasAdhayx: \eng{a rod of variable
 length} udadxvanunx mApaRDisikoLaLx bahudAda salAki. \eng{the
 pressure is variable} otatxDavu badalAyisuvaMthadu. 
\num{2} (kAru \mo vugaLa giyarina \vi) veVgavanunx badalAyisabahudAda. 
\num{3} badalAyisuva parxvaqtitxyuLaLx; asithxra;
caMcal. \eng{variable mood} asithxra manoVvaqtitx. \eng{variable
 fortune} caMcalvAda adaqSaTx, BAgayx. 
\num{4} (gALiya \vi) dikukx badalAyisutatxleV iruva. 
\num{5} (\Kavi) (tAreya \vi) caMcal; kAMtiyu AvataRniVyavAgi badalAguva. 
\num{6} (\ga) cara; (\sA\ biVjgaNitiVya saMkeVtada \vi) vividha
saMKAyxmwlyxviruva; anidiRSaTx mUlyxda. 
\num{7} 
\alnum{a} (\jiVvi\ matutx \savi) (jiVvijAtiya \vi) jAtiya vishiSaTxte

\bentry
\word{vary} 
\pron{veVri} 
\gl{\kirx}(vataRmAna \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{varies}; \BU\ matutx 
\BUkaq\ \eng{varied}). 
{\dictmeaning{}}

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{ 
\num{1} badalAyisu; mApaRDisu; vayxtAyxsagoLisu: \eng{we can vary the
 pressure at will} otatxDavanunx, saMmadaRvanunx, nAvu beVkAdaMte
mApaRDisabahudu. \eng{he seldom varies the routine} dinacariyanunx
avanu badalAyisuvudu tiVra viraLa, bahushaH
badalAyisuvudillx. \eng{the doctor varies the treatment according to
 circumstances} veYdayxnu cikitAsxvidhAnavanunx saMdaBoRVcitavAgi
vayxtAyxsa mADutAtxne. 
\num{2} veYvidhayxgoLisu: \eng{his style is not sufficiently varied}
avana sheYliyalilx sAkaSuTx veYvidhayxvillx.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (guN, rUpa, pariNAma, \mo vugaLalilx) badalAyisu;
badalAvaNeyAgu; vayxtAyxsavAgu: \eng{his mood varies from day to day}
avana manasusx, manaHsithxti dinadiMda dinakekx
badalAyisutitxrutatxde. \eng{the temperature varies from}
\eng{$30^\circ$} \eng{to} \eng{$70^\circ$} tApamAnavu
\eng{$30^\circ$} yiMda \eng{$70^\circ$} ge vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{2} beVreyAgiru; BinanxvAgiru: \eng{this varies from the type} idu
tananx jAtiyiMda BinanxvAgide, beVre bageyadAgide. 
\num{3} beVrebeVreyAgiru; bagebageyAgiru; vividhavAgiru; Binanx
BinanxvAgiru: \eng{opinions vary on this point} I viSayadalilx
aBipArxyagaLu bagebageyAgive, BinanxBinanxvAgive. 
\num{4} anuguNvAgiru; anusAravAgi, anuguNvAgi badalAvaNe hoMdu:
\eng{the demand varies with the season} beVDike kAlkekx
anuguNvAgirutatxde, anuguNvAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{5} (\ga) (anuloVmavAgi yA viloVmavAgi) badalAyisu; Binanx
mwlyxgaLanunx paDe: \eng{attraction of bodies varies directly as their
 masses and inversely as the square of their distance} kAyagaLa
parasapxra AkaSaRNe avugaLa parimANkekx anuloVmavAgi matutx
dUrakekx viloVmavAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde, badalAyisutatxde.}

\bentry
\word[vent(1)]{vent} 
\pron{veMTf} 
\gl{\nA} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (oLahogalu yA horahoraDalu eDegoDuva) terapu; kaMDi; bAyi;
toLe; raMdharx; dAvxra: 

\alnum{a} PiraMgiya hiMBAgadalilx madudx hotitxsuva bAyi. 

\alnum{b} piVpAyiyiMda darxvavanunx horategeyuvalilx piVpAyiyoLakekx
gALi nugagxlu adara meVlgxDe mADiruva raMdharx. 

\alnum{c} OlgadaMtha saMgiVtada vAdayxgaLalilx beraLugaLiMda mucacxlu
tereyalu mADiruva raMdharxgaLalolxMdu. 

\alnum{d} (mane \mo vugaLa CAvaNiya meVlN) hogekaMDi. 

\alnum{e} jAvxlAmuKiya hoge uguLuva bAyi. 
\num{2} (\kanmu\ keLavagaRgaLa pArxNigaLalilx malvisajRna,
saMtAnoVtapxtitxgaLeraDakUkx sAdhanavAda) guda; AsanadAvxra. 
\num{3} (\rUpa) (koVpatApa, asahane, \mo\ BAva, aBipArxya, BAvane, \mo
vanunx horadoVralu yA vayxkatxpaDisalu baLasuva) vidhAna; upAya; dAri;
mAgaR; riVti; avakAsha: \eng{he gave vent to his indignation at such
 injustice} aMtha anAyxyada viSayadalilx avaniguMTAda nAyxyavAda
koVpavanunx avanu vayxkatxpaDisida. \eng{his impatience found a vent
 in his restless conduct} avana caDapaDikeyalilx avana asahane
vayxkatxgoMDitu. 
\num{4} (niVrunAyi \mo\ jlcara pArxNigaLu usirADalu) niVriniMda
horakekx baruvudu.} 
\eentry

\num{2} saTATxvAyxpAra: \eng{one lucky venture made his fortune}
adaqSaTxkaravAda oMdu saTATxvAyxpAra avanige aishavxyaRvanunx
taMdukoTiTxtu. 
\num{3} (\pArxparx) paN; (naSaTxvAdarU AgaleMdu dheYyaRmADi) oDiDxda

\bentry
\word[venture(2)]{venture} 
\pron{venacxrf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (mADuvudu, muMdiDuvudu, maMDisuvudu, paN oDuDxvudu, \mo
vakekx) dheYyaR, sAhasa -- mADu: \eng{he would not venture an opinion}
tananx aBipArxya heVLalu dheYyaR mADalollxde hoVda. \eng{he would not
 venture a guess} avanu Uhe saha mADalu dheYyaR mADalollx. \eng{he
 would not venture a step} avanu oMdu hejejx muMdiDalU dheYyaR
mADalollx. 
\num{2} (paN \mo vanunx oDuDxva, baMDavALa \mo vanunx hUDuva) sAhasa
mADu: \eng{I will venture a bet on it} nAnu adara meVle oMdu paN
oDuDxtetxVne.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} dheYyaRmADu; sAhasamADu; aMjdiru: \eng{I did not venture to
 stop him} avananunx taDeyalu nAnu dheYyaR mADalillx. \eng{I venture
 to differ with you} nimamx aBipArxyakekx BinanxvAda aBipArxyavanunx
sUcisuva sAhasa mADutetxVne. 
\num{2} baralu yA hoVgalu muMtAda sAhasamADu, dheYyaRmADu: \eng{I
 shall not venture out} nAnu horakekx hoVgalu dheYyaR mADuvudillx. 
\num{3} apAyagaLige mununxgugx.}}

\noindent

\num{2} vasaMtavanunx hoVluva; vasaMtasadaqsha: \eng{vernal flowers}
vasaMta kusumagaLu; vasaMtada yA vasaMtakAlda hUvugaLanunx hoVluva
hUvugaLu. 
\num{3} vasaMta(kAl)dalilx naDeyuva yA mADuva: \eng{vernal migration}
vasaMtada valse. \eng{vernal fancies} vasaMtoVcita kalpxnegaLu;
vasaMta Qutuvige takakx kalpxnegaLu.} 
\eentry

\gl{\pagu} 
\eng{the, this, that, his, etc. very} ivaneV, ideV, avaneV, adeV, 
avana savxMta, itAyxdi athaRgaLalilx avadhAraNAthaRdalilx, otitx
heVLuva \parx : \eng{this is the very spot where I found it} nanage
adu doreta sathxLa, ideV. \eng{the very same} tadavxtAtxgi
adeV. \eng{these were his very words} ivu avana savxMta mAtugaLu; I
mAtugaLu avanaveV. \eng{speaking in this very room} I koThaDiyalelxV
mAtanADutAtx. \eng{he did it this very day} avanu adanunx ideV dina,
iMdeV mADida. \eng{the very fact of his presence is enough} avanu
hAjrAgidadx eMba saMgatiyeV sAku. \eng{you are the very man I am
 looking for} nAnu huDukutitxruva vayxkitx niVneV. \eng{a needle is
 the very thing for our purpose} namamx udedxVshakekx beVkAda vasutx
eMdare sUjiyeV. \eng{come here this very minute} I kaSxN(dalelxV)
ililx bA. \eng{it grieves me to the very heart} adu nananx
haqdayAMtarALavanenxV vayxthegoLisutatxde. \eng{the very stones cry

tendencies} durAcAra parxvaqtitxgaLu. \eng{vicious life} pApiSaThx

\num{2} keTTx; keDukina; duSaTx; durAcAra, duraBAyxsagaLige bidadx:
\eng{vicious companions} keTTx, duSaTx -- oDanADigaLu.

doVSagaLuLaLx.

 view} A pakiSx noVTda vAyxpitxge baMtu. \eng{the ship passed from
 our view} A haDagu namamx daqSiTxyiMda sariyitu,
kaNmxreyAyitu. 
\num{4} noVT; daqshayx; nidiRSaTx sAthxnadiMda
noVDalpxTTxdudx: \eng{the house has a view of the sea} A maneyiMda
samudarxda noVT sigutatxde, samudarx kANutatxde. \eng{a superb view}
aduBxtavAda oMdu noVT, Bavayxdaqshayx. 
\num{5} daqshayxcitarx; yAvudeV vasutx \mo vugaLa noVTvanunx
oLagoMDiruva citarx. 
\num{6} daqSiTx; aBipArxya; BAvane; yAvudeV viSayavanunx -- noVDuva
bage, kurita manoVBAva: \eng{he takes a different view} avanu beVre
aBipArxyavanunx taLedidAdxne. \eng{his view is that we are aggressors}
nAvu AkarxmaNkArareMbaudu avana BAvane. \eng{that is his view of her
 conduct} avaLa naDavaLikeya viSayadalilx avana daqSiTx adu. \eng{he
 holds extreme views (in politics etc. )} (rAjkiVya \mo vugaLalilx)
avanu tiVvarxgAmi aBipArxyagaLanunx hoMdidAdxne. \eng{took a
 favourable view of the matter} viSayada bagegx anukUlkara aBipArxya
taLeda. 
\num{7} udedxVsha; Ashaya; eNike: \eng{will this meet your views?} idu
nimamx udedxVshagaLige sarihoMdutatxdeye? 
\num{8} viVkaSxN; avaloVkana; pariVkaSxN; samIkaSxN; cAkuSxSa yA
mAnasika samiVkeSx; kaNiNxniMda yA mAnasikavAgi pariVkiSxsuvudu,
taniKe mADuvudu. 
\num{9} viVkaSxN; viVkaSxNAvakAsha: \eng{a view of the exhibition}
parxdashaRnada viVkaSxNe, noVT.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{have in view} 

\alnum{a} (yAvudanenxV) guriyanAnxgi, udedxVshavanAnxgi hoMdiru. 

\alnum{b} (tiVmARnisuvAga, yAvudeV aMshavanunx) gamanadalilx,
daqSiTxyalilx -- iTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{2} \eng{in view of} 

\alnum{a} daqSiTxpathadalilx yA pathakekx; kaNiNxge biVLuva sAthxnadalilx: 
\eng{we came in view of the church} A cacuR kaNiNxge biVLuva
sAthxnakekx baMdevu. 
\eng{he stood in view of the audience} avanu perxVkaSxkara
daqSiTxpathadalilx niMta. 

\alnum{b} daqSiTxyiMda; noVDidare; noVDidalilx; gamanisidare;
parigaNisidare; kAraNdiMda: 
\eng{in view of the recent developments, we do not think this step
 advisable} ititxVcina GaTnegaLanunx 
noVDidare, parigaNisidare, I hejejx (kAyaRkarxma) vihitavAdadedxMdu
namage toVruvudillx. 

\alnum{c} (\pArxparx) (muMde Aguvudanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx adakekx)
pUvaRBAviyAgi. 
\num{3} \eng{on view} noVDuvudakAkxgi, pariVkeSxgAgi, parishiVlnegAgi,
avaloVkanakAkxgi -- parxdashiRsida.
\num{4} \eng{private view} (citarx parxdashaRnada \vi) (senxVhitaru,
vimashaRkaru, \mo) ApatxvagaRkekx mAtarx parxdashaRna; KAsagi
parxdashaRna. 
\num{5} \eng{take a \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{dim(1) nuga}{${}^1$dim} view of.}
\num{6} \eng{take a \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{poor pagu(3)}{poor} view of.}
\num{7} \eng{take the long-term view of} (yAvudeV \vi) dUrAloVcane
mADu; BaviSayxvanunx ciMtisu. 
\num{8} \eng{to the view} bahiraMgavAgi; parxtayxkaSxvAgi;
parxkaTvAgi; ellxrigU kANuvaMte. 
\num{9} \eng{with a view to} 

\alnum{a} udedxVshadiMda yA niriVkeSxyiMda; guriyatatx oMdu hejejxyAgi. 

\alnum{b} (yAvudanenxV) paDeyuvudakAkxgi; (meVle) kaNiNxTuTx;
paDeyuvudakokxVsakxra; paDeyuva saluvAgi: 
\eng{with a view to marriage} maduveya saluvAgi, daqSiTxyiMda.}

\bentry 
\word[vital(1)]{vital} 
\pron{veYT(Tf)lf} 
\gl{\gu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} jeYvika; jiVvadhAraka; jiVvanAdhAravAda; badukige, badukuva 
kirxyege, jiVvakirxyege yA jiVvavAyxpArakekx saMbaMdhisida yA
atAyxvashayxkavAda: \eng{vital energies} jeYvikashakitxgaLu;
ceYtanayxgaLu. \eng{vital functions} jeYvika -- kirxyegaLu,
vAyxpAragaLu. \eng{wounded in a vital part} mamaRsAthxnadalilx,
jiVvashakitxyu atisUkaSxmXvAgiruva sathxLadalilx -- gAyagoMDa. 
\num{2} (yAvudeV vasutxvina uLivige yA keYgoMDiruva viSayakekx)
pArxNAdhAravAda; atAyxvashayxkavAda; atimuKyxvAda: \eng{a vital
 question or question of vital importance} atimuKyxvAda parxshenx,
viSaya. \eng{secrecy is vital to the success of the scheme} I
yoVjneya yashasisxge goVpayxte atimuKyx, atayxgatayx. 
\num{3} pArxNda, jiVvada -- meVle pariNAmavuLaLx. 
\num{4} mAraka; pArxNAMtaka; jiVvakekx, pArxNkekx yA yAvudeV kAyaRda
jyakekx -- mArakavAda: \eng{a vital wound} mArakavAda gAya. \eng{a
 vital error} (jyakekx, saPaltege) mArakavAda tapu px, doVSa. 
\num{5} jiVvaMta; sajiVva; jiVvaMtikeyiMda kUDida, tuMbida;
ceYtanayx, caTuvaTike -- tuMbida. 
\num{6} (vivAda parxyoVga) muKyx; parxdhAna.}

niVDiruva A padagaLa paTiTx.

\word{vocation} 
\pron{vakeVSa(Sf)nf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} ahaRtABAvane; nidiRSaTx udoyxVga yA vaqtitxge tAnu
 takakxvaneMba, tanage ahaRteyideyeMba daqDhaBAvane.  
\num{2} deYvaperxVraNe; deVvAdiSaTxvAda vaqtitx; deYva saMkalipxta
kAyaR yA sithxti; deYvaperxVritaveMdu BAvitavAda vaqtitx yA udoyxVga:
\eng{he felt no vocation for the ministry} pAdirxvaqtitxge avanalilx
deYvaperxVraNeyiralillx. 
\num{3} (aMtaH)perxVraNe; parxvaqtitx; olvu: \eng{he has no vocation
 to literature} avanige sAhitayxracaneyatatx olvillx,
 parxvaqtitxyillx.  
\num{4} (\kanmu\ sharxdedhx toVrabeVkeMdu parigaNitavAda) vayxkitxya 
-- vaqtitx, kasubau, udoyxVga. 
\num{5} yAvudeV udoyxVga, vaqtitx, kasubau.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\eng{mistook his vocation} tanage ogugxva vaqtitx hiDiyalillx,
tiLiyalillx.}

\bentry 
\word[voice(1)]{voice} 
\pron{vAyfsx} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (dhavxninALadalilx huTiTx bAyalilx horaDuva, \kanmu\
manuSayxra) dhavxni; dani; shabadx; kaMTha; gaMTlu: \eng{I heard a
 voice} nanage oMdu dhavxni keVLisitu. \eng{he spoke in a low voice}
avanu meludaniyalilx mAtanADida. \eng{I did not recognize her voice}
nanage Akeya dhavxniya guruteV sigalillx. \eng{the voice of the
 cuckoo} koVkil dhavxni; koVkilkaMTha. \eng{he has such a loud voice}
avanige aSoTxMdu gaTiTxyAda dhavxni ide. 
\num{2} 
\alnum{a} (mAtina \vi) ucAcxraNe. 

\alnum{b} (hADina \vi) kaMTha; shAriVra. 
\num{3} gaMTlu; kaMTha; dhavxni(shakitx); shAriVra(bal): \eng{has lost
 her voice} avaLa shAriVra kugigxhoVgide. 
\num{4} mAtu; dani; nAlige; vAkukx; vANi; \kanmu\ ADida yA bareda
padagaLu: \eng{he gave voice to his indignation 
in a pamphlet} avanu oMdu kiruhotatxgeyalilx tananx nAyxyavAda
koVpavanunx padagaLalilx horageDahida, koVpakekx nAlige koTTx. 
\eng{the dog gave voice to its joy} A nAyi tananx AnaMdavanunx
kUginalilx sUcisitu. 
\num{5} 
\alnum{a} mAtu; dhavxni; vayxkatxpaDisida aBipArxya. 

\alnum{b} aBipArxya koDuva hakukx: \eng{I have no voice in this
 matter} I viSayadalilx nanage aBipArxya koDuva hakikxllx. 

\alnum{c} vANi; aBipArxya vayxkatxpaDisalu baLasuva vayxkitx yA
sAdhana. 
\num{6} (\dhavxni) GoVSavaNR; dhavxnitaMtugaLa anuraNnadiMda yA
kaMpanadiMda huTuTxva dhavxni. 
\num{7} (\vAyx) (kirxyApadada) kataRri, kamaRNi yA BAveV -- parxyoVga
rUpa; kataRqvigU kirxyegU iruva saMbaMdhavanunx 
sUcisuva kirxyArUpagaLalilx oMdu. 
\num{8} 
\alnum{a} (\saM) saMgiVta kaqtiya hADuva yA gAyana BAga. 

\alnum{b} (\saM) PUZyxgf eMba saMgiVta kaqtiya gAyanAMsha. 
\num{9} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) deYvavANi; ashariVra, agoVcara -- dhavxni;
adaqshayx Atamxvu mAgaRdashaRna mADalu 
nuDidudeMdu naMbalAda mAtu, dhavxni, shabadx.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{at the \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{top(1)16}{${}^1$top} of one's voice.}
\num{2} \eng{in (good) voice} 

\alnum{a} (mAtanADuvudaralilx) oLeLxya ucAcxraN shakitxyuLaLx. 

\alnum{b} (hADuvudaralilx) (utatxma) kaMThavuLaLx, shAriVravuLaLx. 
\num{3} \eng{the voice of God} deYvavANi; deYva -- saMkalpx; korxVdha,
shApa, \mo vugaLa aBivayxkitx. 
\num{4} \eng{with one voice} EkakaMThadiMda; EkABipArxyadiMda;
okokxraliniMda; omamxtadiMda.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[vote(1)]{vote} 
\pron{voVTf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} voVTu; (aBi)mata; aBayxthiRyanunx Ayekx mADuvudu, kAnUnanunx
maMjUru mADuvudu, TharAvanunx opu pxvudu, \mo\ saMdaBaRgaLalilx
matadAna patarxda meVle gurutisuvudu, keYetutxvudu, kUguvudu yA
beVrAvudeV riVtiyalilx niVDuva aBipArxya: \eng{I shall give my vote
 to (\engit{or} for) the Labour candidate} nAnu kAmiRka pakaSxda aBayxthiRge
yA aBayxthiRya paravAgi nananx mata niVDutetxVne. \eng{the resolution
 was put to the vote and passed without a dissent vote} A
TharAvanunx voVTige hAkalAgi Binanxmatavillxde opapxlAyitu. 
\num{2} (\birx)

\alnum{a} (sakARravu koVrida haNda \vi) (pAliRmeMTina) bahumatada anumoVdane. 

\alnum{b} bahumatABipArxya; bahumatadiMda vayxkatxvAda aBipArxya. 
\num{3} voVTugaLa, matagaLa -- motatx; (oMdu pakaSx \mo vu yA oMdu
pakaSx \mo vakekx koTTx yA koDabahudAda oTuTx voVTugaLu): 
\eng{he will lose the Labour vote} avanu kAmiRka pakaSxda matagaLanunx
kaLedukoLuLxvanu. 
\num{4} (\kanmu\ rAjyxda cunAvaNeyalilx) matAdhikAra; matadAnada,
voVTu mADuva -- hakukx: \eng{Swiss women now have the vote} 
sivxTZsxlRMDina heMgusarige Iga voVTina, voVTumADuva hakikxde. 
\num{5} voVTu ciVTi; voVTnunx gurutisalu baLasuva kAgada \mo vu.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{put to a (\engit{or} the) vote} matakekx hAki niNRyisu,
niNRyakekx oDuDx yA opipxsu. 
\num{2} \eng{take a vote on} (yAvudeV viSayada bagegx) mata tegeduko;
(yAvudanenxV) matadAnada mUlka niNRyisu. 
\num{3} \eng{vote of censure} = \hyperlink{vote1 pagu5}{\pagu \eng{(5)}.} 
\num{4} \eng{vote of confidence} vishAvxsa mata; ADaLita pakaSxvanunx
adhikasaMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvareMdu toVrisuva bahumata. 
\hypertarget{vote1 pagu5}{}
\num{5} \eng{vote of no confidence} avishAvxsa mata; ADaLita
pakaSxvanunx adhika saMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvudilalxveMdu sUcisuva
bahumata.}

yA samiti \mo vugaLa sadasayxtavxdiMda vajAmADu:
